							<div class="mw-indicators">
		<div id="mw-indicator-pp-default" class="mw-indicator"><div class="mw-parser-output"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Protection_policy#semi" title="This article is semi-protected until November 10, 2026 at 16:52 UTC, due to vandalism"><img alt="Page semi-protected" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/1/1b/Semi-protection-shackle.svg/20px-Semi-protection-shackle.svg.png" decoding="async" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/1/1b/Semi-protection-shackle.svg/40px-Semi-protection-shackle.svg.png 1.5x" data-file-width="512" data-file-height="512" /></a></span></div></div>

						<div id="siteSub" class="noprint">From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia</div>
					</div>
					<div id="contentSub"><div id="mw-content-subtitle"></div></div>
					
					
					<div id="mw-content-text" class="mw-body-content"><div class="mw-content-ltr mw-parser-output" lang="en" dir="ltr"><p class="mw-empty-elt">
</p>
<style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r1236090951">.mw-parser-output .hatnote{font-style:italic}.mw-parser-output div.hatnote{padding-left:1.6em;margin-bottom:0.5em}.mw-parser-output .hatnote i{font-style:normal}.mw-parser-output .hatnote+link+.hatnote{margin-top:-0.5em}@media print{body.ns-0 .mw-parser-output .hatnote{display:none!important}}</style><div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Not to be confused with <a href="/wiki/List_of_countries_by_GDP_(nominal)" title="List of countries by GDP (nominal)">List of countries by GDP (nominal)</a>.</div>
<link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1236090951"><div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">For countries by GDP per capita, see <a href="/wiki/List_of_countries_by_GDP_(PPP)_per_capita" title="List of countries by GDP (PPP) per capita">List of countries by GDP (PPP) per capita</a>.</div>
<p class="mw-empty-elt">
</p><p class="mw-empty-elt">
</p>
<table border="0" cellpadding="2" cellspacing="0" style="float:right;">

<tbody><tr>
<td><div class="timeline-wrapper"><map name="timeline_kmi6ynnjcb3rgmasunsy4l5gnp8tept"></map><img usemap="#timeline_kmi6ynnjcb3rgmasunsy4l5gnp8tept" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/timeline/kmi6ynnjcb3rgmasunsy4l5gnp8tept.png"></div>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align:center; font-size:90%;">Largest economies in the world by GDP (PPP) in 2025<br>according to <a href="/wiki/International_Monetary_Fund" title="International Monetary Fund">International Monetary Fund</a> estimates<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-1"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>1<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</td></tr></tbody></table>
<figure typeof="mw:File/Thumb"><a href="/wiki/File:GDP_PPP_2024_Selection.svg" class="mw-file-description"><img src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5c/GDP_PPP_2024_Selection.svg/330px-GDP_PPP_2024_Selection.svg.png" decoding="async" width="270" height="244" class="mw-file-element" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5c/GDP_PPP_2024_Selection.svg/500px-GDP_PPP_2024_Selection.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5c/GDP_PPP_2024_Selection.svg/960px-GDP_PPP_2024_Selection.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1089" data-file-height="985"></a><figcaption>Selection of GDP PPP data (top 10 countries and blocs) in no particular order</figcaption></figure>
<p>GDP (PPP) means <a href="/wiki/Gross_domestic_product" title="Gross domestic product">gross domestic product</a> based on <a href="/wiki/Purchasing_power_parity" title="Purchasing power parity">purchasing power parity</a>.  
This article includes a list of countries by their forecast estimated GDP (PPP).<sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>2<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> Countries are sorted by GDP (PPP) forecast estimates from financial and statistical institutions that calculate using market or government official <a href="/wiki/Exchange_rate" title="Exchange rate">exchange rates</a>. The data given on this page are based on the <a href="/wiki/Geary%E2%80%93Khamis_dollar" class="mw-redirect" title="Geary–Khamis dollar">international dollar</a>, a standardized unit used by economists. Certain regions that are not widely considered countries such as <a href="/wiki/Hong_Kong" title="Hong Kong">Hong Kong</a> also show up in the list if they are distinct jurisdiction areas or economic entities.  
</p><p>GDP comparisons using PPP are arguably more useful than those using <a href="/wiki/List_of_countries_by_GDP_(nominal)" title="List of countries by GDP (nominal)">nominal GDP</a> when assessing the domestic market of a state because PPP takes into account the relative cost of local goods, services and inflation rates of the country, rather than using international market exchange rates, which may distort the real differences in per capita income.<sup id="cite_ref-ICP_3-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ICP-3"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>3<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> For example, while the nominal GDP ranks of Germany and India are third and fourth respectively, when adjusted for PPP Germany's GDP drops to sixth and India rises to third because the local cost of goods in India is lower, and thus same nominal amount of money can buy more goods and services in India.
</p><p>GDP adjusted for PPP, however, is limited when measuring financial flows between countries and when comparing the quality of same goods among countries.<sup id="cite_ref-CallenIMF_4-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CallenIMF-4"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>4<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> PPP is often used to gauge global <a href="/wiki/Poverty_threshold" title="Poverty threshold">poverty thresholds</a> and is used by the <a href="/wiki/United_Nations" title="United Nations">United Nations</a> in constructing the <a href="/wiki/Human_Development_Index" title="Human Development Index">Human Development Index</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-ICP_3-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ICP-3"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>3<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> These surveys such as the International Comparison Program include both tradable and non-tradable goods in an attempt to estimate a representative basket of all goods.<sup id="cite_ref-ICP_3-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ICP-3"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>3<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p><p>The first set of data on the left columns of the table includes estimates for the year 2023 made for each economy of the 196 economies (189 <a href="/wiki/United_Nations" title="United Nations">U.N.</a> member states and 7 areas of <a href="/wiki/Aruba" title="Aruba">Aruba</a>, <a href="/wiki/Hong_Kong" title="Hong Kong">Hong Kong</a>, <a href="/wiki/Kosovo" title="Kosovo">Kosovo</a>, <a href="/wiki/Macau" title="Macau">Macau</a>, <a href="/wiki/Palestine" title="Palestine">Palestine</a>, <a href="/wiki/Puerto_Rico" title="Puerto Rico">Puerto Rico</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Taiwan" title="Taiwan">Taiwan</a>) covered by the <a href="/wiki/International_Monetary_Fund" title="International Monetary Fund">International Monetary Fund</a> (IMF)'s <a href="/wiki/International_Financial_Statistics" class="mw-redirect" title="International Financial Statistics">International Financial Statistics</a> (IFS) database. The data is in millions of international dollars and was calculated and published by the IMF in October 2023. The second table includes data, mostly for the year 2022, for 180 of the 193 current <a href="/wiki/United_Nations_member_states" class="mw-redirect" title="United Nations member states">United Nations member states</a> as well as Hong Kong and <a href="/wiki/Macau" title="Macau">Macau</a> (the two Chinese <a href="/wiki/Special_administrative_regions_of_China" title="Special administrative regions of China">Special Administrative Regions</a>). Data are in millions of international dollars; they were compiled by the <a href="/wiki/World_Bank" title="World Bank">World Bank</a>. The third table is a tabulation of the <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.cia.gov/the-world-factbook/field/real-gdp-purchasing-power-parity/country-comparison">CIA World Factbook GDP (PPP)</a> data update of 2019. The data for GDP at purchasing power parity has also been rebased using the new International Comparison Program price surveys and extrapolated to 2007. Non-sovereign entities (the world, continents, and some <a href="/wiki/Dependent_territory" title="Dependent territory">dependent territories</a>) and <a href="/wiki/List_of_states_with_limited_recognition" title="List of states with limited recognition">states with limited recognition</a> (such as <a href="/wiki/Kosovo" title="Kosovo">Kosovo</a>, <a href="/wiki/Palestine" title="Palestine">Palestine</a> and Taiwan) are included in the list in cases in which they appear in the sources. These economies are not ranked in the charts here, but are listed in sequence by GDP for comparison. In addition, non-sovereign entities are marked in <style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r981673959">.mw-parser-output .legend{page-break-inside:avoid;break-inside:avoid-column}.mw-parser-output .legend-color{display:inline-block;min-width:1.25em;height:1.25em;line-height:1.25;margin:1px 0;text-align:center;border:1px solid black;background-color:transparent;color:black}.mw-parser-output .legend-text{}</style><span class="legend-color mw-no-invert" style="background-color:#F0E891; color:black;">&nbsp;yellow&nbsp;</span>.
</p>
<meta property="mw:PageProp/toc">
<div class="mw-heading mw-heading2"><h2 id="Table">Table</h2></div>
<p><i>The table is initially ranked by the average of the available estimates for each country or territory, and can be reranked by any of the sources.</i>
</p><p><i>The links in the "Country/Territory" row of the following table link to the article on the GDP or the economy of the respective country or territory.</i>

<table class="wikitable sortable sticky-header-multi sort-under static-row-numbers" style="text-align:right;">
<caption>GDP (millions of <a href="/wiki/Real_and_nominal_value" title="Real and nominal value">current</a> <a href="/wiki/International_dollar" title="International dollar">international dollar</a>) by country or <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r981673959"><span class="legend-color mw-no-invert" style="background-color:#F0E891; color:black;">&nbsp;territory&nbsp;</span>
</caption>
<tbody><tr class="static-row-header" style="text-align:center;vertical-align:bottom;">
